     390           0 : static int canonical_ranking(an_il_entry_kind  kind,

     392             : /*

     395             : powers of 2 for various binary criteria (some of which apply only to
     396             : certain kinds of entities.  The criteria are (in increasing order of
     397             : importance):
     398             :    (a) Is the entity's parent canonical?
     399             :    (b) Is the entity in the primary IL?
     400             :    (c) Does the entity have an explicit initializer? (variables only)
     401             :        Does the entity have a determined exception specification?
     402             :                                                      (routines only)
     403             :    (d) Is the entity a template specialization?
     404             :        If it is a prototype instantiation, is the associated template
     405             :        defined?
     406             :    (e) Is the entity defined?
     407             :    (f) Is the entity a non-weak definition or (for a type) complete?
     408             : The entity with the highest ranking in a correspondence set should be the
     409             : canonical entry.  (See also corresp_ranking in trans_copy.c for a reduced
     410             : version of this function.)
     411             : The given entity should have a source correspondence.
